On the **Eleventh Day**, the Heavenly Worthy of Disaster-Dispelling and Calamity-Resolving descends.

On the **Thirteenth Day**, the Heavenly Thearch of Grand Simplicity descends.

On the **Fifteenth Day**, the Western Dipper descends; the Perfected Lord Chongsu ascends as an immortal.

On the **Sixteenth Day**, the Southern Dipper descends; the Perfected Lord Pan Zizhen ascends as an immortal.

On the **Seventeenth Day**, Perfected Lord Zhao Guangxin ascends. On the **Nineteenth Day**, the Northern Yin descends. On the **Twentieth Day**, the Heavenly Strategist descends. On the **Twenty-Second Day**, Perfected Lord Zhang Yuanhua ascends. On the **Twenty-Fourth Day**, the Southern Dipper descends. On the **Twenty-Fifth Day**, the Heavenly Penetrator descends. On the **Twenty-Seventh Day**, the Northern Dipper descends. On the **Twenty-Eighth Day**, the Ten Directions’ Savior-from-Suffering Heavenly Worthies descend. On the **Twenty-Ninth Day**, Perfected Consort Jiuhua of Tongbai Mountain manifests; the Northern Yin descends.

**Seventh Month**
On the **First Day**, the Festival of Primordial Heaven: the Supreme Venerable Lord ascends to the Great Ultimate to pay homage to the Celestial Worthy of Original Beginning and the Great Emperor; the Seven Star Lords of the Western Quarters descend.
On the **Second Day**, the Heavenly Bureau of Plundered Remnants descends.
On the **Third Day**, the Northern Culmen and Northern Dipper descend.
On the **Fifth Day**, the Heavenly Penetrator descends.
On the **Sixth Day**, the Jade Pivot Assembly is established to ensure a month of peace.
On the **Seventh Day**, Prince Qiao of Zhou Lingwang ascends as an immortal; the Southern Dipper descends; the Western Dipper descends; the Perfected Warrior descends. The Queen Mother of the West and the Upper Lady of the Primordial manifest before Emperor Wu of Han; the Nine Heavens’ Responsive Primordial Guardian of Destiny manifests; the Great Immortal Magu and Perfected Lord Wang Fangping descend; Perfected Lord Fuqiu Shao ascends.
On the **Ninth Day**, the Eastern Dipper descends; the Northern Yin descends.
On the **Tenth Day**, the Heavenly Worthy of Longevity and Life-Preservation descends.
On the **Eleventh Day**, the Heavenly Worthy of Disaster-Dispelling and Calamity-Resolving descends.
On the **Fifteenth Day**, the Day of Earthly Bureau Pardon for Sins and the Festival of Heavenly Perfected Qian-Yuan: on this day, Perfected Lord Shi Lingwei saves his mother in Northern Fengdu. On this day, Dao practitioners set up altars, commissioning Daoist masters to perform Offering Rites to deliver and uplift the departed, ascending them to the Heavenly Realm.
On the **Sixteenth Day**, Immortal Official Zhang Yuanchong ascends as an immortal; the Heavenly Bureau of Plundered Remnants descends.
On the **Eighteenth Day**, Perfected Lord Wei Chuyuan ascends as an immortal; the Great Possessor Mother descends.
On the **Nineteenth Day**, the Heavenly Strategist descends.
On the **Twenty-Third Day**, Perfected Lord Yu Wengsheng ascends.
On the **Twenty-Fourth Day**, the Sagely Attendant descends; the Northern Dipper sets forth on a tour.
On the **Twenty-Fifth Day**, the Heavenly Penetrator descends.
On the **Twenty-Seventh Day**, the Heavenly Thearch tours the Eastern Well; the Northern Culmen and Northern Dipper descend.
On the **Twenty-Eighth Day**, Perfected Lord Liu of Western Luo ascends as an immortal.
On the **Twenty-Ninth Day**, the Heavenly Perfected Sovereign receives the *Six Wang Formula Charts*, the *Six Jia Three Primordials Concealment Arts*, and the *Secret Classic of Formula-Making* from the Yellow Emperor of Xuanyuan; the Northern Yin descends.

**Eighth Month**
On the **First Day**, the Day of Pursuing Sweetness: Perfected Lord Yin Taihe ascends as an immortal.
On the **Second Day**, the Three Primordials of Grand Simplicity pay homage to the Perfected; the Heavenly Bureau of Plundered Remnants descends.
On the **Third Day**, the Northern Culmen and Northern Dipper descend; the Sagely Attendant Perfected Lord descends.
On the **Fifth Day**, the Heavenly Emperor of Thunder descends; Perfected Lord Zhu the Youth ascends.
On the **Seventh Day**, the Western Dipper descends.
On the **Eighth Day**, the Heavenly Worthy of Grand Compassion and Savior-from-Suffering descends; the Southern Dipper descends.
On the **Ninth Day**, the Festival of Primordial Completion: the Azure Florescence Emperor Lord descends; the Eastern Dipper descends; the Northern Yin descends.
On the **Tenth Day**, the Heavenly Worthy of Longevity and Life-Preservation descends.
On the **Eleventh Day**, the Heavenly Worthy of Disaster-Dispelling and Calamity-Resolving descends; the Grand Dipper sets forth on a tour.
On the **Thirteenth Day**, the Perfected Warrior descends.
On the **Fifteenth Day**, the Supreme Ultimate Jade August Thearch, the Great Matriarch Wuyi, and the Perfected Lord of Manifest Dao descend; the Yellow Emperor of Xuanyuan mounts a dragon to ascend; the Divine Merit and Wondrous Salvation Perfected Lord Xu, together with his household, ascends on the forty-second day; Perfected Lord Zhang Chen ascends with his household.
On the **Sixteenth Day**, the Heavenly Bureau of Plundered Remnants descends.
On the **Seventeenth Day**, the Star Lord of Venus descends; the Southern Dipper descends.
On the **Eighteenth Day**, the Dragon Kings of the Four Seas convene in the East.
On the **Nineteenth Day**, the Northern Dipper sets forth on a tour; the Sagely Attendant descends; Perfected Lord Tian Shiwen and Celestial Master Shen ascend as immortals.
On the **Twenty-First Day**, the Heavenly Strategist descends.
On the **Twenty-Second Day**, the Southern Dipper descends.
On the **Twenty-Fourth Day**, Perfected Lord Qian Hui Peng ascends with his household.
On the **Twenty-Fifth Day**, the Heavenly Penetrator descends.
On the **Twenty-Sixth Day**, the Old Man of the Southern Culmen, the Star of Longevity, manifests.
On the **Twenty-Seventh Day**, the Northern Culmen and Northern Dipper descend; the Sagely Attendant descends.
On the **Twenty-Eighth Day**, the Four Heavens offer summer’s return to the origin.
On the **Twenty-Ninth Day**, the Northern Yin descends.

**Ninth Month**
On the **First Day**, the Supreme Dao Lord convenes the *Anthology of Spirits* in the Jade Radiance Numinous Chamber of the Golden Palace of the Jade Firmament, meeting with the Eastern Florescence Azure Emperor; the Southern Dipper descends. The Three Primordials of Grand Simplicity pay homage to the Perfected.
On the **Third Day**, the Nine Mounds Earthly August Lords ascend to the Wavering Pear Realm to memorialize the cultivators of Dao and virtue from the Nine Lands before the Lords of the Four Heavens; the Northern Culmen and Northern Dipper descend; the Illustrious Sagely descends.
On the **Fourth Day**, the Thunder Gods of the Five Directions descend.
On the **Sixth Day**, the Jade Pivot Assembly is established to ensure a month of peace.
On the **Seventh Day**, the Western Dipper descends.
On the **Ninth Day**, the Day of Longevity Extension: the Supreme Jade Radiance Great Dao Lord ascends to the Jade Firmament’s Forest Chamber of the Four Celestial Terraces; the Eastern Dipper descends; the Northern Culmen descends; the Eastern Florescence Emperor Lord manifests; the Supreme Savior-from-Suffering Heavenly Worthy descends; the Perfected Warrior ascends as an immortal; the Three Heavens’ Upholder of the Dao, Assistant of the Mysterious, Great Dharma Master, Orthodox Unity, and Quiescent Responsive Perfected Lord—the First Celestial Master of the Han Dynasty—along with Perfected Lord Wang of the Jade Treasury, Perfected Lord Zhao the Right Attendant, and Perfected Lord Xu the Left Minister ascend as immortals.
On the **Eleventh Day**, the Heavenly Worthy of Great Compassion and Great Mercy universally saves all beings of the Three Realms, delivering them from suffering and calamity; the Heavenly Worthy of Disaster-Dispelling and Calamity-Resolving descends.
On the **Fifteenth Day**, the Western Dipper descends.
On the **Sixteenth Day**, the Heavenly Bureaus record the names of the living and the dead; the Heavenly Bureau of Plundered Remnants descends.
On the **Nineteenth Day**, the Day of Union between the Palaces of Sun and Moon and the Yin-Yang Palace: the stellar deities of the various heavens and the Radiant Worthy of Upper Clarity each illuminate their respective palaces; the Northern Dipper Heavenly Emperor descends to the mortal realm to register the lifespans of humans and record their good and evil deeds; the Sagely Mother of the Northern Yin descends.

On the **Twentieth Day**, the Heavenly Emperor tours the Eastern Well.
On the **Twenty-First Day**, the Heavenly Strategist descends.
On the **Twenty-Fifth Day**, the Southern Dipper descends; the Heavenly Penetrator descends.
On the **Twenty-Seventh Day**, the Northern Culmen and Northern Dipper descend.
On the **Twenty-Ninth Day**, the Sagely Mother of the Northern Yin descends.

**First Day of the Tenth Month**, the Day of All Things’ Completion: the Eastern August Emperor’s birthday; Perfected Lord Wang Chang manifests; the Seven Stellar Lords of the Northern Palace descend; Celestial Master Ma Yuanjue ascends.
On the **Third Day**, the Northern Dipper descends; the Dragon Kings of the Four Seas and Nine Rivers gather in the Water Caverns to present their memorials.
On the **Fourth Day**, Perfected Lords Xia Qing, Gui Qing, Zhanran, Penglai, and Miaoran manifest.
On the **Fifth Day**, the Heavenly Penetrator descends.
On the **Sixth Day**, the Heavenly Bureaus and the Five Marchmount Emperors register the records of life; on this day, the Jade Pivot Assembly is established to ensure a month of peace.
On the **Seventh Day**, the Western Dipper descends.
On the **Ninth Day**, the Eastern Dipper descends; the Northern Yin descends.
On the **Tenth Day**, the Heavenly Worthy of Great Compassion Who Saves from Suffering descends; the August Guardian descends; the Northern Dipper begins its procession; the Heavenly Worthy Who Preserves Life and Protects Destiny descends; the Perfected King of Divine Empyrean and Jade Clarity descends.
On the **Eleventh Day**, the Heavenly Worthy of Disaster-Dispelling and Calamity-Resolving descends.
On the **Thirteenth Day**, the Southern Dipper descends.
On the **Fifteenth Day**, the Lower Prime Day: one may perform the Dao and establish fasts to cultivate the self and repent transgressions; the Water Emperors of the Nine Rivers, the Great Spirits of the Twelve River Sources and Valley Streams, the Divine King of the Sunlit Valley, and the Numinous Officials of the Water Palaces descend together to the mortal realm to assess merits and transgressions; the Water Official of the Lower Prime descends to inspect good and evil deeds; the Western Dipper descends.
On the **Eighteenth Day**, the Day of Memorials Presented to the Three Heavens: the Heavenly Emperor tours the Eastern Well.
On the **Nineteenth Day**, the Northern Yin descends.
On the **Twentieth Day**, Perfected Lord Xuanling Tonghua descends.
On the **Twenty-First Day**, the Heavenly Strategist descends; the Perfected Warrior descends.
On the **Twenty-Fourth Day**, the Festival of the Descending Sage: the Sagely Mother and Heavenly Worthy Who Protects Life manifests.
On the **Twenty-Fifth Day**, the Festival of Heavenly Talismans: the Southern Culmen and Heavenly Worthy of Long Life and Great Empyrean manifests; the Heavenly Penetrator descends.
On the **Twenty-Sixth Day**, the Southern Dipper descends; the August Guardian descends; the Northern Dipper begins its procession.
On the **Twenty-Seventh Day**, the August Emperor of Purple Tenuity and Northern Culmen descends; the Northern Dipper descends.
On the **Twenty-Ninth Day**, the Northern Yin descends.

**First Day of the Eleventh Month**: Perfected Lord Wang Hongfan ascends; the Northern Dipper begins its procession; Lord Ge the Immortal receives the Golden and Water Scriptures of the Three Heavens from the Great Unity.
On the **Second Day**, the Heavenly Bureau of Plundered Remnants descends.
On the **Third Day**, the Supreme Jade Dawn Great Dao Lord ascends to the Jade Empyrean and Glittering Chamber to survey the world below; the Northern Culmen descends; the Southern Dipper descends.
On the **Fifth Day**, the Festival of Heavenly Response: the gods and immortals of the suburban sacrifices descend; the Heavenly Penetrator descends.
On the **Sixth Day**, the Jade Pivot Assembly is established to ensure a month of peace.
On the **Seventh Day**, the Perfected Warrior descends.
On the **Ninth Day**, the Eastern Dipper descends; the Southern Dipper descends; the Northern Dipper begins its procession.
On the **Tenth Day**, the Heavenly Worthy Who Preserves Life and Protects Destiny descends.
On the **Eleventh Day**, the Heavenly Worthy of Great Mercy universally saves all beings of the Three Realms, delivering them from suffering and calamity; the Heavenly Worthy of Disaster-Dispelling and Calamity-Resolving descends.
On the **Fourteenth Day**, the Five Emperors descend.
On the **Fifteenth Day**, the Day of Blessing-Initiation: the Heavenly Emperor tours the Eastern Well; the Western Dipper descends.
On the **Sixteenth Day**, the Heavenly Bureau of Plundered Remnants descends.
On the **Seventeenth Day**, the Heavenly Bureau of Plundered Surplus descends to oversee the evil deeds of mortals; the Northern Dipper descends.
On the **Nineteenth Day**, the Great Dharma Masters of the Three Heavens subdue the twenty-four cavern spirits and gods of Shu.
On the **Twenty-First Day**, the Heavenly Strategist descends.
On the **Twenty-Third Day**, the Six Stellar Lords of the Southern Dipper present the registers of life; the Thunder Gods of the Five Directions descend.
On the **Twenty-Fourth Day**, the Southern Dipper descends.
On the **Twenty-Fifth Day**, the Northern Dipper begins its procession; the Heavenly Penetrator and August Guardian descend.
On the **Twenty-Sixth Day**, the Heavenly Worthy of Lofty Perfection and Wondrous Fruit manifests.
On the **Twenty-Seventh Day**, the Northern Culmen and Northern Dipper descend.
On the **Twenty-Eighth Day**, Perfected Lord Yongwu Shi ascends.
On the **Twenty-Ninth Day**, the Northern Yin descends.

**First Day of the Twelfth Month**: the multitude of immortals convenes at Penglai.
On the **Third Day**, the Lord of the Kitchen and Controller of Destiny, together with the Supreme Perfected of the Jade Capital and Great Culmen and the Azure Lad of the Eastern Sea, manifests; the Heavenly Bureau of Plundered Remnants descends.
On the **Fourth Day**, the Nine Mound Earth Sovereigns ascend to the Heavenly Court to present the names of those who study virtue and the Dao in the Nine Lands, becoming lords of the Four Heavens.
On the **Fifth Day**, the Heavenly Penetrator descends.
On the **Sixth Day**, the Jade Pivot Assembly is established to ensure a month of peace.
On the **Seventh Day**, the Western Dipper descends.
On the **Ninth Day**, the Eastern Dipper descends; the August Guardian descends; the Northern Yin descends.
On the **Tenth Day**, the Heavenly Worthy Who Preserves Life and Protects Destiny descends.
On the **Eleventh Day**, the Heavenly Worthy of Great Mercy universally saves all beings of the Three Realms, delivering them from suffering and calamity; the Heavenly Worthy of Disaster-Dispelling and Calamity-Resolving descends.
On the **Seventeenth Day**, the Left Auxiliary of Supreme Mystery and Essence and the Lady of Great Unity descend to the Golden Altar of Crooked Hook.
On the **Eighteenth Day**, the Grand Master of the Three Teachings, the Supreme Lord Lao, the August Emperor of Primordial Virtue and Chaos, manifests.
On the **Nineteenth Day**, the Northern Yin descends; the Thunder Gods of the Five Directions descend.
On the **Twentieth Day**, the Perfected Lord August Guardian descends; the Northern Dipper begins its procession.
On the **Twenty-First Day**, the Perfected of the Various Heavens pay homage to the Primordial Three Clarities; the Five Strategists descend; Perfected Lord Nanji Chongxu meets the immortals.
On the **Twenty-Second Day**, the Heavenly Worthy Who Protects the State and Brings Peace descends.
On the **Twenty-Third Day**, the Envoys of the Nine Heavens, the Heavenly Officials of the Three Primes Who Examine and Verify, the Judges of the Five Directions’ Thunder Departments, the Numinous Officials of the Five Marchmounts, and the King of Fengdu who Surveys the Dark Capital descend to assess the merits and transgressions of mortals over the year. Those of great filial piety and loyalty have their lifespans extended by three cycles and their families prosper for three generations. Those who perform hidden meritorious deeds have their lifespans extended and their families prosper according to their merits. Those who perform great acts of kindness for others have their lifespans extended by one year and their families prosper for one generation for each act; a hundred acts bring prosperity for a hundred generations. Those who eliminate harm to bring peace to the multitude have their lifespans extended by one year for each harm removed. Judicial officials who save ten from death have their lifespans extended by one year; ordinary people who save one from death have their lifespans extended by one cycle. Those who abandon the Dao of Heaven, turn their backs on the August Emperor of the Supreme Heaven, destroy the Perfected of the Various Heavens, and extinguish the Dao of the Middle Kingdom are reborn as beasts in the great borderlands, never to return to human form or be born in the Middle Land.

All descendants—children, grandchildren, nephews, and nieces—who are unfilial toward their grandparents, parents, uncles, or aunts shall be struck down by the Thunder Department, their lifespans shortened by three cycles and their forms extinguished. Those who commit kin-slaying shall have their lifespans reduced by two cycles under the Thunder Department’s decree. Those who disrupt harmony among the six relations shall have their lifespans shortened by one cycle. Ministers, servants, or slaves who defy their lords or deceive their sovereigns shall be slain by the Wind Blade, their lifespans reduced by three cycles. Those who usurp blessings or indulge in excess shall face the desecration of their coffins and the severing of their reputations, suffering punishment even after death, with their descendants reduced to beggary and extinction. Rebels who sow chaos, commit treason, and slaughter the innocent shall have their nine clans exterminated and their nine generations of ancestors afflicted. Thieves and murderers shall have their souls severed by ghosts, repaying their crimes within one cycle across three lifetimes. Those who kill surrendered generals or soldiers shall have their lifespans forfeited by Heaven, their forms annihilated by the myriad spirits, dying without descendants; their nine clans shall suffer calamity, repaying their crimes for a hundred generations. Judicial officials who cause even one death shall be sent to the Pestilence Bureau’s Department of Malignant Diseases, their lifespans shortened by two cycles and their crimes repaid in one lifetime; if they cause five deaths, they shall be swiftly extinguished, repaying their crimes for five lifetimes, with three generations of ancestors afflicted. Ordinary people who cause one death shall be sent to the Northern Feng, their lifespans shortened by one cycle and their crimes repaid in one lifetime; if the victim does not die, their lifespans shall be reduced by five years.

On the twenty-fourth day, the Three Realms convene in assembly, the Deities of Destiny ascend to court, and the Northern Culmen descends.
On the twenty-fifth day, the Three Pure Ones and the Jade Emperor hold a joint assembly, and Tianpeng descends.
On the twenty-seventh day, the Northern Culmen and the Northern Dipper descend, Zhenwu descends, and the Southern Culmen’s Miao Dao Zhenjun receives the Dao from the Universal Salvation Zhenjun.
On the twenty-eighth day, the Most High Lord Lao transforms the thirty-six kinds of heterodox demons and foreign spirits, subduing them; the Northern Dipper emerges on its procession.
On the twenty-ninth day, the Perfected of the Three Realms embark on their victorious sojourn.
On the thirtieth day, the Deities of Destiny descend to the mortal realm.

**Three Assembly Days**
The seventh day of the first month is called the Assembly of Promotion and Reward. On this day, the Upper Prime bestows blessings, and the Heavenly Official, together with the Earth and Water Officials, reviews merits and transgressions.
The seventh day of the seventh month is called the Middle Assembly of Celebrating Life. On this day, the Middle Prime grants amnesty, and the Earth Official, together with the Heaven and Water Officials, reviews merits and transgressions.
The fifteenth day of the tenth month is called the Grand Assembly of Establishing Life. On this day, the Lower Prime dispels misfortune, and the Water Official, together with the Heaven and Earth Officials, reviews merits and transgressions.
On these Three Assembly Days, the Three Officials examine deeds and misdeeds, and the three souls gather to report the good and evil of the living. These days are also called the Three Souls’ Assembly Days, when one should burn incense and repent of transgressions.

**Three Prime Days**
The fifteenth day of the first month is the Upper Prime, the fifteenth day of the seventh month is the Middle Prime, and the fifteenth day of the tenth month is the Lower Prime.
On these Three Prime Days, the deities of the Heaven, Earth, and Water Officials—twenty-seven bureaus and one hundred twenty offices—first review merits and transgressions on the Three Assembly Days, then ascend to the Golden Gates to report, thereby determining blessings and calamities. On these days, one may practice the Dao, establish fasts, cultivate the self, and repent of transgressions.

**Eight Seasonal Nodes**
**Beginning of Spring:** The Most High Heavenly Worthy of the Northeast, together with the Lord of the Primordial Azure Qi of the Brahma-Heaven, descends.
**Spring Equinox:** The Most High Heavenly Worthy of the Jade Treasure Star of the East, together with the Lord of the Nine Qi of the Azure Emperor, descends.
**Beginning of Summer:** The Heavenly Worthy of the Southeast, Who Nurtures Life and Delivers Destiny, together with the Lord of the Primordial Vermilion Qi of the Brahma-Heaven, descends.
**Summer Solstice:** The Heavenly Worthy of the Mysterious Truth and Myriad Blessings of the South, together with the Lord of the Three Qi of the Vermilion Emperor, descends.
**Beginning of Autumn:** The Most High Heavenly Worthy of the Grand Void of the Southwest, together with the Lord of the Primordial White Qi of the Brahma-Heaven, descends.
**Autumn Equinox:** The Most High Heavenly Worthy of the Supreme Mystery of the West, together with the Lord of the Seven Qi of the White Emperor, descends.
**Beginning of Winter:** The Boundless Heavenly Worthy of the Grand Florescence of the Northwest, together with the Lord of the Primordial Mysterious Qi of the Brahma-Heaven, descends.
**Winter Solstice:** The Most High Heavenly Worthy of the Mysterious Jade Dawn of the North, together with the Lord of the Five Qi of the Black Emperor, descends.
On these days, the Heavenly Worthies of the Eight Directions and the Lords of Qi descend to the mortal realm to record human merits and transgressions and observe good and evil.

**Five La Days**
The first day of the first month is called Heavenly La. On this day, the Five Emperors convene in the Azure Heaven of the Nine Qi of the East.
The fifth day of the fifth month is called Earthly La. On this day, the Five Emperors convene in the Vermilion Heaven of the Three Qi of the South.
The seventh day of the seventh month is called Moral La. On this day, the Five Emperors convene in the White Heaven of the Seven Qi of the West.
The first day of the tenth month is called People’s Year La. On this day, the Five Emperors convene in the Black Heaven of the Five Qi of the North.
The eighth day of the eleventh month is called Lords’ and Marquises’ La. On this day, the Five Emperors convene in the Mystic Capital and Jade Metropolis of the Upper Realm.
On these days when the Five Emperors gather, the Heavenly Emperor of the Northern Feng of Fengdu reviews the souls of the dead and examines the good and evil deeds of the ancestors of the living and their present descendants to determine blessings and calamities. These days weigh upon the living, who should perform offerings and give thanks, relying on the power of the Dao to perform rituals, redeem suffering, and secure blessings in every respect. Ordinary days are not suitable for such sacrifices.

**Three Nodal Days**
Heavenly Node: Jiawu
Earthly Node: Jiachen
Human Node: Jiazi

**Eight Assembly Days**
Heavenly Assembly: Bingwu
Earthly Assembly: Renwu
Human Assembly: Renzi
Solar Assembly: Gengwu
Lunar Assembly: Gengshen
Stellar Assembly: Xinyou
Five Agents Assembly: Jiachen
Four Seasons Assembly: Jiaxu
On these nodal and assembly days, one should fast, burn incense, perform offerings to the stars, recite scriptures, make repentances, and sacrifice to ancestral spirits to extend one’s lifespan and increase one’s allotted years.

**Days for Offerings to the Stars**
Spring: Jiazi, Jisi
Summer: Dingchou, Bingchen
Autumn: Xinhai, Gengzi
Winter: Guiwei, Renyin
The first, third, fifth, seventh, ninth, fifteenth, seventeenth, twenty-first, twenty-fifth, and twenty-seventh days of the month are suitable for making offerings to the stars and petitioning the Dipper.

**Days of Merit Review**
On Jiazi, Taiyi inspects the gods and spirits.
On Gengshen, the Three Corpses report human merits and transgressions.
On one’s natal day, one’s deeds are tallied.
On these days of merit review, the Radiant Spirit of the Womb reports to the Luminous Spirit on Jiazi, the Obscure Essence reports on Gengshen, and one’s natal day is when one’s good and evil deeds are reported. On these days, one should receive talismans, fast, present memorials, and make petitions to pray for great blessings.

On the full moon day, it is fitting to pay homage, repent sins, pray for blessings, and give thanks for past transgressions.

**Six Fasting Days**
The eighth, fourteenth, fifteenth, twenty-third, twenty-ninth, and thirtieth days of the month.
Food is not eaten after noon.

**Three Short Fasting Days**
The eighth, fifteenth, and thirtieth days of the month.
Food is not eaten after noon.

**Six Ding Fasting Days**
The *Spring and Autumn Mandate and Sincerity Chart* states: The Yellow Emperor inquired of Taiyi about the Dao of long life, and Taiyi replied, "Fast on the six Ding days, and you may achieve success."
The *Inner Transmission* states: The Emperor swore to vanquish Chiyou, then fasted for three days to report to the Supreme Deity. This was the beginning of fasting and abstinence.

**Ten Straight Fasting Days**
According to the *Old唐书*, Zhou Boyangfu transmitted this fast to the king of Tanyao, Fan Tuo Ali, who observed these ten fasts within a month.
- On the first day, contemplate the Infinite Great Florescence Heavenly Worthy, repent the transgression of killing and harming living beings, and avoid the retribution of inverted hanging and butchery.
- On the eighth day, contemplate the Jade Clarity Heavenly Worthy of the Mysterious Upper Realm, repent the transgression of defying principle and pursuing selfishness, and avoid the retribution of golden hammers and iron staves.
- On the fourteenth day, contemplate the Heavenly Worthy of Transcendent Sagely Salvation, repent the transgression of harming others for personal gain, and avoid the retribution of iron beds and copper pillars.
- On the fifteenth day, contemplate the Heavenly Worthy of the Jade Treasure Emperor, repent the transgression of relying on strength to bully the weak, and avoid the retribution of flying spears and drifting halberds.
- On the eighteenth day, contemplate the Heavenly Worthy of Life-Nurturing Salvation, repent the transgression of self-deception in the heart, and avoid the retribution of intestines pierced and tongues plowed.
- On the twenty-third day, contemplate the Heavenly Worthy of Mysterious Perfection and Myriad Blessings, repent the transgression of flattery to the face and slander behind the back, and avoid the retribution of swallowing fire and eating coals.
- On the twenty-fourth day, contemplate the Heavenly Worthy of the Great Numinous Empty Sovereign, repent the transgression of delusion and bewilderment, and avoid the retribution of cauldrons of boiling water and furnaces of coals.
- On the twenty-eighth day, contemplate the Heavenly Worthy of the Supreme Wondrous Ultimate, repent the transgression of willfully committing evil, and avoid the retribution of ice spears and frost blades.
- On the twenty-ninth day, contemplate the Heavenly Worthy of the True Sovereign and Cavern Spirit, repent the transgression of mistakenly injuring benevolence, and avoid the retribution of burning and scorching.
- On the thirtieth day, contemplate the Heavenly Worthy of the Jade Void Luminous Sovereign, repent the transgression of karmic retribution across the Three Realms, and avoid the retribution of bellies pierced and hearts blocked.

Emperor Gaozong said: Che Yin told Hu monks that all were translated from Sanskrit, with "Heavenly Worthy" as "Buddha" and "karmic retribution" as "hell," thus establishing the ten fasts.

**Fasting in the First, Fifth, and Ninth Months**
According to Dou Ping’s *Phonetic and Exegetical Notes on the Old唐书*, its annotation on Emperor Gaozu’s decree to refrain from executions in the first, fifth, and ninth months states: The Heavenly Emperor created the Great Treasure Mirror to illuminate the Four Great Continents, moving it each month to observe human good and evil. In the first month, the mirror shines on the Southern Jambu Continent; in the second, on the Eastern Victory Continent; in the third, on the Northern Uttarakuru Continent; in the fourth, on the Western Godaniya Continent; in the fifth, again on the Southern Jambu Continent. Rotating thus, the first, fifth, and ninth months all shine upon the Southern Jambu Continent. Therefore, in these three months, criminal laws are reviewed, and taxes and levies are reduced. Since the Sui and Tang dynasties, this has been recorded in the legal codes. During these three months, executions and slaughter are prohibited. Later generations, following the Tang precedent, withheld mutton stipends from officials during these months due to the prohibition on executions and slaughter. In truth, this custom originated in the Tang dynasty, and later generations transmitted it as fasting in the first, fifth, and ninth months. Those with discernment call this the act of the most foolish, while those with even slight wisdom regard such practices as base and shameful. Since the Song dynasty, the Daoist tradition has abolished them.

The Ten "Imperial Execution" Days and Monthly Taboos
On these days, burning incense is forbidden; violators forfeit their allotted lifespan.
First month: the second day and *gengshen*; second month: the ninth day and *xinyou*; third month: the tenth day and *gengxu*; fourth month: the eleventh day and *guihai*; fifth month: the eleventh day and *renzi*; sixth month: the tenth day and *guichou*; seventh month: the twelfth day and *jiayin*; eighth month: the thirteenth day and *yimao*; ninth month: the thirteenth day and *bingchen*; tenth month: the eighth day and *dingsi*; eleventh month: the fifteenth day and *bingwu*; twelfth month: the thirteenth day and *dingwei*.

Heavenly Taboo Days
*Bingyin* and *dingmao*: taboo for Daoist fathers; *bingshen* and *dingyou*: taboo for Daoist mothers; *renchen* and *renxu*: taboo for the Northern Emperor; *wuchen* and *wuxu*: taboo for the Southern Emperor. Days of severed fate and one’s own fate-star; days when Jupiter transits the year’s position; days when the Six Harmful Stars align with one’s fate-star; the last three days of the lunar month; days of annual rupture and yearly clash.

Laozi’s Hair-Restoration Days
First month: the fourth day; second month: the eighth day; third month: the eleventh day; fourth month: the sixteenth day; fifth month: the twentieth day; sixth month: the twenty-fourth day; seventh month: the twenty-eighth day; eighth month: the nineteenth day; ninth month: the sixteenth day; tenth month: the thirteenth day; eleventh month: the tenth day; twelfth month: the seventh day.

In the thirty-fifth year of the Wanli reign of the Great Ming, cyclical year *dingwei*, on an auspicious day of the Upper Yuan, Zhang Guoxiang, Orthodox Successor of the Zhengyi Tradition, Perfected of Sincere Constancy, Who Propagates the Dao and Expounds the Mysteries, Great Perfected Who Governs the Daoist Teachings Throughout the Realm, by imperial decree oversaw the carving of the printing blocks.

Chapter on Numerical Records of Affairs
Heavenly patterns and earthly configurations, the transformations of yin and yang, the official systems of past and present, rituals and human affairs, systems of caps and robes, music, classics and histories, literary works, elixir arts, medicine, and implements—all are recorded by number. Given the vastness of these categories, it is impossible to exhaust them; only one or two items currently needed by the Mystery Gate are selected, their essentials compiled and arranged below as essential knowledge for Daoist practitioners.

One Number
One Principle.

The Supreme Ultimate.
One Greatness.
The realm of kings contains Four Greatnesses, and the king occupies one of them. Called the Most Revered.

Two Numbers
Two Modes: Heaven, Earth.
Two Luminaries: Sun, Moon.
Two Qi: Yin, Yang.
Two Worthy Ministers of Shang: Laozi, Pengzu.
Two Elders of Shang: Taigong, Boyi.
Two Parents: Father, Mother.

Three Numbers
Three Primes: Supreme Beginning, Supreme Simplicity, Supreme Origin.
Three Powers: Heaven, Earth, Humanity.
Three Realms: Heaven, Earth, Water. (Some say: Upper, Middle, Lower.)
Three Lights: Sun, Moon, Stars.
Three Heavens: Qingwei Heaven, Yuyu Heaven, Taichi Heaven.
Three Purities and Three Realms:
Jade Purity Sacred Realm, where the Primordial Beginning resides;
Upper Purity True Realm, where the Dao Lord resides;
Grand Purity Immortal Realm, where the Old Lord resides.
Three Treasures: Dao, Scriptures, Master.
Three August Ones of Antiquity: Heavenly Sovereign, Earthly Sovereign, Human Sovereign.
Three Enclosures: Purple Tenuity Enclosure, Supreme Tenuity Enclosure, Heavenly Market Enclosure.
Three Terraces: Upper Terrace, Middle Terrace, Lower Terrace.
Three Departments: Supreme Mystery Capital Department, Heavenly Pivot Department, Heavenly Mechanism Department.
Three Thunder Departments:
Heavenly Master Zhang presides over the Capital Department,
Immortal Ge presides over the Mystery Department,
Perfected Lord Xu presides over the Supreme Department.
Floating Hill’s Three Immortals oversee the affairs of the Three Departments.
Three Masters: Heavenly Master Zhang Daoling, Successor Master Zhang Heng, Lineage Master Zhang Lu.
(Also said: Scripture Master, Registry Master, Ordination Master.)
Three Qi: Beginning Qi (green), Original Qi (white), Mysterious Qi (black).
Three Flowers: Golden Flower, Jade Flower, Ninefold Flower.
Three Caverns: Cavern of Truth, Cavern of Mystery, Cavern of Spirit.
Three Antiquities: High Antiquity (Fuxi’s time), Middle Antiquity (King Wen of Zhou’s time), Low Antiquity (Confucius’ time).
Three Vehicles: Great Vehicle, Middle Vehicle, Small Vehicle.
Three Sovereigns: Great Fuxi of Taihao, Flame Emperor Shennong, Yellow Emperor Xuanyuan.
Three Masters’ Texts: Laozi’s *Dao De Jing*, Zhuangzi’s *Nanhua Jing*, Liezi’s *Chongxu Jing*.
Three Stars of Great Fire: Central Star, Fore Star, Rear Star.
Three Norms: Zi as Heavenly Norm, Chou as Earthly Norm, Yin as Human Norm.
Three Dawns: Dawn of the Year, Dawn of the Month, Dawn of the Day.
Three Beginnings: Early Dawn, Cock’s Crow, Midnight.
Three Fasts: Initial Fast, Middle Fast, Final Fast.
Three Earth Altars: Grand Earth Altar, Royal Earth Altar, Bo Earth Altar.
Three Commanding Festivals: First day of the first month, Third day of the third month, Ninth day of the ninth month.
Three Origins: Upper Origin, Middle Origin, Lower Origin.
Three Assemblies: Seventh day of the first month (Heavenly Assembly), Seventh day of the seventh month (Earthly Assembly), Fifteenth day of the tenth month (Water Assembly).
Three Lords Mao:
Eldest Lord Mao, named Ying;
Second Lord Mao, named Gu;
Youngest Lord Mao, named Zhong.
Three Mountain Registers:
Upper Purity Register from Mount Mao,
Numinous Treasure Register from Mount Gezao,
Orthodox Unity Register from Mount Longhu.
Three Sacred Mountains:
Mount Penglai (also called Peng Hu),
Mount Fangzhang (also called Fang Hu),
Mount Yingzhou (also called Ying Hu).
Three Islands in the Sea: Fusang Island, Penglai Island, Kunlun Island—all dwellings of immortals.
Three Mountains of Numinous Light:
Mount Emei, where the Palace of the Heavenly Perfected Sovereign once stood (usurped by Li Xiong of the Five Hu as a Hu temple);
Mount Lu, where the Palace of the Great Bright Lord once stood (monk Huiyuan petitioned the prefect of Jiangzhou, Huan Yi, to seize the Heavenly Pond Hermitage and Tiger Brook Shrine, converting them into Hu temples);
Mount Wutai, where the Palace of the Purple Mansion’s Yanmen Lord once stood (usurped by Liu Yuan of the Five Hu as a Hu temple).
Three Water Palaces:
Upper Water Palace of Mount Madang, ruled by King Fushan Anjiang;
Middle Water Palace of Mount Caishi, ruled by King Shunsheng Pingjiang;
Lower Water Palace of Mount Jin, ruled by King Zhaoxin Taijiang.
Three River Lords: Lord of the Luo River, Lord of the Yellow River, Lord of the Huai River.
Three Passes: Mouth as Heavenly Pass, Feet as Earthly Pass, Hands as Human Pass.
Three Elixir Fields: Upper Elixir Field, Middle Elixir Field, Lower Elixir Field.
Three Hun: Taiguang, Shuangling, Youjing.
Three Flowers: Essence, Qi, Spirit.
Three Daoist Chariots:
Gathering fire to circulate qi with the heart, used to cure illness—called the Messenger’s Chariot;
Yin and yang unite, water and fire merge, thunderous sounds heard in stillness—called the Thunder Chariot;
The heart enslaved by external realms, qi scattered by sensory impressions, leading to aging and illness—called the Broken Chariot.
Three River Chariots:
Gathering medicine, advancing fire, adding mercury, drawing lead—called the Small River Chariot;
The great medicine gradually forms, refining above and below—called the Great River Chariot;
Returning the elixir, refining the body, merging with the Dao to become an immortal—called the Purple River Chariot.
Three Medical Chariots:
The Ox Chariot (qi ascends from the tailbone to the Muddy Pellet Palace);
The Deer Chariot (small intestine and bladder circulate minor water);
The Goat Chariot (large intestine circulates major waste).
Three Corpses (also called Three Pengs):
Upper Corpse Peng Ju, named Green Maiden, attacks the eyes, dwells in the head, incites excessive desires and love of carriages and horses;
Middle Corpse Peng Zhi, named White Maiden, attacks the five viscera, dwells in the abdomen, incites gluttony and quick temper;
Lower Corpse Peng Qiao, named Blood Maiden, attacks the stomach and life, dwells in the feet, incites lust and fondness for killing.
Three Paths (also called Three Evils):
Gate of Sensual Desire, the path of the Upper Corpse—Heavenly Realm Boundary;
Gate of Attachment, the path of the Middle Corpse—Human Realm Boundary;
Gate of Greed, the path of the Lower Corpse—Earthly Realm Boundary.
Three Longevities:
Upper Longevity: one hundred years;
Middle Longevity: eighty years;
Lower Longevity: sixty years.
(Also said: Upper Longevity: one hundred twenty years; Middle Longevity: one hundred years; Lower Longevity: eighty years.)
Three Fungi: Stone Fungus, Numinous Fungus, Flesh Fungus.

Four Numbers
Four Qi: Heaven, Earth, Sun, Moon.
Four Realms: Heavenly Realm, Earthly Realm, Water Realm, Yang Realm.
Four Greatnesses in the Realm: Dao Great, Heaven Great, Earth Great, King Great.
Four Images: Greater Yang, Lesser Yang, Greater Yin, Lesser Yin.
Four Gratitudes: Heaven and Earth, the King, the Master, Parents.

Four Poles:
Eastern Florescence, Southern Culmen, Western Numinosity, Northern Perfection.

Four Assistants:
Grand Perfection, Grand Peace, Grand Purity, Orthodox Unity.

Four Seasons:
Spring, Summer, Autumn, Winter.

Four First Months:
First Month of Spring, First Month of Summer, First Month of Autumn, First Month of Winter.

Four Mid-Months:
Mid-Spring, Mid-Summer, Mid-Autumn, Mid-Winter.

Four Final Months:
Final Month of Spring, Final Month of Summer, Final Month of Autumn, Final Month of Winter.

Four Qi:
Spring as Green Yang, Summer as Vermilion Brightness, Autumn as White Storehouse, Winter as Dark Obscurity.

Four Heavens:
Spring as Azure Heaven, Summer as Vast Heaven, Autumn as Brilliant Heaven, Winter as Supreme Heaven.

Four Palaces:
Spring as the Palace of Generating Beings, Summer as the Palace of Growing Beings, Autumn as the Palace of Gathering Beings, Winter as the Palace of Storing Beings.

Fire for the Four Seasons:
In spring, fire from elm and willow;
In summer, fire from jujube and apricot;
In the final month of summer, fire from mulberry and cudrania;
In autumn, fire from oak and catalpa;
In winter, fire from locust and sandalwood.

Four Directions:
East, West, South, North.

Four Corners:
Southeast, Southwest, Northeast, Northwest.

Four Wastelands:
Eastern Mouth Below, Queen Mother of the West, Southern North Region, Northern Bamboo Raft.

Four Outer Limits:
Southward from Jizhou to where the sun is overhead, forming the Crimson Waters and completing wisdom;
Northward to where the Dipper and Pole Star are overhead, forming Kongtong, its people martial and stalwart;
Eastward to where the sun rises, forming the Great Peace and awaiting arrival;
Westward to where the sun sets, forming the Great Vastness, Primal Vastness, and Great Auspiciousness.

Four Extremities:
East to Taiyuan, South to Puzhou, West to Bin State, North to Zhuli.

Four Barbarians:
Eastern Yi, Western Rong, Southern Man, Northern Di.

Four Virtues of Heaven:
Origin, Prosperity, Benefit, Integrity.

Four Offices of Heavenly Ministries:

Four Offices of Earthly Ministries:

Four Mountains in the Sea:
Mount Penglai, in the Eastern Sea.
Mount Fusang, in the Eastern Sea.
Mount Fangzhang, in the Great Sea.
Mount Canglang, in the Great Sea.

Four Dragon Kings of the Seas:
Dragon King of the Eastern Sea Water Palace, Eastern Sea of Laizhou.
Dragon King of the Southern Sea Water Palace, Southern Sea of Guangnan.
Dragon King of the Western Sea Water Palace, Western Sea of Jiangzhong Prefecture.

Four River Source Kings:
King of the Broad Source of the Jiang River, Jianning County;
King of the Numinous Source of the He River, Longmen County;
King of the Long Source of the Huai River, Mount Tongbai;
King of the Clear Source of the Ji River, Jiyuan County.

Four Sacred Beasts:
Azure Dragon Emperor Lord Mengzhang,
White Tiger Emperor Lord Guardian of the Army,

Dark Warrior Emperor Lord Holder of Light.

Dong Shuangcheng,
Xu Feiqiong,
Wan Linghua,
Duan Anxiang.

Four Essentials of Nurturing Life:
Reduce thought to nourish the spirit,
Reduce desire to nourish essence,
Reduce labor to nourish strength,
Reduce speech to nourish qi.

Four Virtues:
Benevolence, Righteousness, Propriety, Wisdom.

Four Beginnings:
Compassion, Deference, Shame, Discernment of Right and Wrong.

Four Considerations:
The day’s plan lies in the morning,
The year’s plan lies in spring,
The life’s plan lies in diligence,
The family’s plan lies in oneself.

Four Good Foundations of Conduct:
Read good books,
Associate with good people,
Speak good words,
Do good deeds.

Five Numerals:
Five Ultimates.

Primordial Void, Primordial Non-Being, Primordial Simplicity, Primordial Substance, Primordial Pole.

The Five Colors:
Blue-Green, Red, Yellow, White, Black.

The Five Measures:
Year, Month, Day, Calendar, Stars.

The Five Directions:
East, West, South, North, Center.

The Five Constants:
Benevolence, Righteousness, Propriety, Wisdom, Trustworthiness.

The Five Notes:
Gong, Shang, Jiao, Zhi, Yu.

The Five Grains:
Millet, Hemp, Beans, Wheat, Legumes.

The Five Lands:
Hills, Mounds, Plains, Lowlands, Burial Grounds.

The Five Phases:
Metal, Wood, Water, Fire, Earth.

The Five Fortunes:
Longevity, Wealth, Health and Peace, Love of Virtue, Natural End of Life.

The Five Officials:
Ears, Eyes, Mouth, Nose, Heart.

The Five Orifices:
Eyes, Tongue, Mouth, Nose, Ears.

The Five Fluids:
The liver produces tears, the heart produces sweat, the spleen produces saliva, the lungs produce mucus, the kidneys produce spittle.

The Qi of the Five Viscera:
Liver qi is frozen, heart blood follows, spleen qi is warm, lung qi is hot, kidney qi is cold.

The Governance of the Five Viscera:
The heart governs smell, the liver governs color, the spleen governs taste, the lungs govern sound, the kidneys govern fluids.

The Storage of the Five Viscera:
The heart stores the spirit, the liver stores the ethereal soul, the spleen stores intention, the lungs store the corporeal soul, the kidneys store the will.

The Connections of the Five Viscera:
The heart connects to the tongue, the liver connects to the eyes, the spleen connects to the mouth, the lungs connect to the nose, the kidneys connect to the ears.

The Preferences of the Five Viscera in Illness:
Heart illness favors delirious speech, liver illness favors shouting, spleen illness favors singing, lung illness favors weeping, kidney illness favors groaning.

The Primordial Qi of Heaven and Earth:
In the east, it divides into blue-green nine; in the south, it receives cinnabar three; in the west, it forms white seven; in the north, it returns to black five; in the center, it governs yellow one.

The Five Kalpas Corresponding to the Five Phases:
Dragon Han belongs to Wood, Red Brightness belongs to Fire, One Sovereign belongs to Earth, Extended Peace belongs to Metal, Kaihuang belongs to Water.

The Five Palaces:
In the east, Ruizhu; in the west, Biyu; in the north, Qinghua; in the south, Ningshen; in the center, Changsheng.

The Five Sacred Peaks:
East Peak Mount Tai, West Peak Mount Hua, South Peak Mount Heng, North Peak Mount Heng, Central Peak Mount Song.

The Five Emperors of the Five Directions:
Azure Emperor Ling Weiyang, Vermilion Emperor Chi Biaonu, White Emperor Bai Zhaoju, Black Emperor Xie Guangji, Yellow Emperor Han Shuniu.

The Five Lake Lords:
Qingcao Lake Water Spirit, Taihu Lake Water Spirit, Danyang Lake Water Spirit, Xie Lake Water Spirit.

The Five Patriarchs:
Lord Donghua, Zhongli Quan, Lü Chunyang, Liu Haichan, Wang Chongyang.

The Five Immortals:
First, Heavenly Immortals; second, Earthly Immortals; third, Divine Immortals; fourth, Human Immortals; fifth, Ghost Immortals.

The Five Grades of Daoists:
Heavenly Perfected Daoists, such as Gao Xuanhuang; Divine Immortal Daoists, such as Du Zhongyi; Mountain-Dwelling Daoists, such as Xu You and Chao Fu; Renunciant Daoists, such as Song Lun and Peng Chen; Householder Daoists, such as Huang Qiong and Qian Keng.

The Five Powers:
Loyalty and filial piety to ruler and parents, rectifying oneself and engaging with things, compassionately saving all beings, putting others before oneself, moderating flavors and abstaining from meat.

The Five Sufferings—Five Corpse Afflictions:
First, the suffering of color accumulation at the heart’s gate; second, the suffering of love accumulation at the spirit’s gate; third, the suffering of greed accumulation at the body’s gate; fourth, the suffering of floral competition at the essence’s gate; fifth, the suffering of bodily accumulation at the ethereal soul’s gate.

The Five La Days:
First day of the first month, Celestial La; fifth day of the fifth month, Earthly La; seventh day of the seventh month, Dao and Virtue La; first day of the tenth month, People’s Year La; La day of the twelfth month, King and Marquis La.

The Five Zhi:
Longbo Zhi resembling intertwined dragons, Shencheng Zhi red and luminous, Yanjv Zhi purple in color, Yeguang Zhi visible at night like moonlight, Yuzhi lustrous as jade.

The Six Numerals:
The Six Harmonies.

Heaven, Earth, east, west, south, north.
The Six Relations:
Father, mother, elder brother, younger brother, wife, child.

The Six Qi:
Yin, yang, wind, rain, darkness, brightness.
The Six Treasuries:
Metal, wood, water, fire, earth, grain.

The Six Offices of the Southern Dipper:
Tianshu, Tianji, Silu, Siming, Tianliang, Tiantong.

The Six Qi:
In spring, consume morning mist; in autumn, consume twilight yin; in winter, drink night vapor; in summer, consume true yang—combined with the primal qi of heaven and earth as the Six Qi.

The Six Spirits:
Heart spirit Danyuan, liver spirit Longyan, spleen spirit Changzai, lung spirit Pohua, kidney spirit Xuanming, gallbladder spirit Longyao.

The Six Breaths:
"Si" governs the lungs, "Xu" governs the heart, "Hu" governs the liver, "Chui" governs the young, "Xi" governs the kidneys, and the Triple Burner.

The Six Viscera:
Gallbladder, stomach, large intestine, small intestine, bladder, Triple Burner.

The Six Qi:
Taiyang cold water, Taiyin damp earth, Shaoyang ministerial fire, Shaoyin sovereign fire, Yangming dry metal, Jueyin wind wood.

The Six Paths:
Heavenly path, human path, demonic path, hell path, hungry ghost path, animal path.

The Six Heavenly Palaces of Fengdu:
Zhoujue Yintian Palace, Taisha Liangshi Zongtian Palace, Mingchen Naifan Wucheng Palace, Huzhao Zuiqi Palace, Songling Qifei Palace, Gansi Lianwanlü Palace.

The Six Offices:
High Master, Chief Lector, Supervisor of Fasts, Scripture Attendant, Incense Attendant, Lamp Attendant.

The Six Hours:
Yin, mao, si, wu, shen, you.

The Number Seven:
Seven Stars of the Northern Dipper: Greedy Wolf, Great Gate, Store of Emolument, Literary Brilliance, Integrity and Chastity, Martial Brilliance, Breaking Army.

Seven Perfected:
Ma Yu, Tan Chuduan, Liu Chuxuan, Qiu Chuji, Wang Chuyi, Hao Datong, Sun Bu’er.

Daoist Benefits:
Scriptural Dharma, Discourse and Debate, Longevity and Purity, Literary Composition for Imperial Command, Ritual Burning, Vocal Praise, Daoist Ritual Codes.

Seven Corporeal Souls:
Corpse Constrainer, Bowel Croucher, Yin Overseer, Heavenly Thief, Rank Poison, Filth Remover, Foul Purity.

The Number Eight:
Eight Winds:
Northwest Unyielding Wind, Northern Vast Desert Wind, Eastern Bright Multitude Wind, Valley-Making Wind, Northeast Melting Wind (also called Twig Wind), Southeast Clear Brightness Wind, Southern Triumphant Wind (also called Capital Wind), Western Closing Gate Wind, Southwest Cool Wind.

Tang Eight Immortals:
Heavenly August Perfected, Master Guangcheng, Master Hongya, Qian Keng, Master Red Pine, Master Yu Feng, Master Ma Shi, Chi Jiang Ziyu.
All were men of the Yellow Emperor’s time. By the era of Tang Yao, the eight roamed Mount Zhongnan, where people saw them and, because it was the age of Tang Yao, called them the Tang Eight Immortals. Later generations mistakenly applied the name to the Eight Immortals of the Tang Li dynasty, such as Lü Dongbin.

Huainan Eight Masters:
Su Fei, Li Shang, Zuo Wu, Tian You, Jin Chang (two names missing, their identities lost; later people erroneously substituted two others).

Prince An of Huainan, grandson of Emperor Gaozu and son of Prince Chang of Huainan, was fond of Confucian learning, esoteric arts, and the methods of divine transcendence and flying ascent. He composed the *Inner Book of Huainan* in twenty scrolls, the *Book of Vast Treasures and Myriad Years* in three scrolls, and the *Fire Lotus Sutra* in five scrolls, expounding the principles of Heaven’s Dao and the transformations of creation, thereby attaining the Way of long life and enduring vision. Each year, he refined three hundred *yi* of yellow gold, offering it to the imperial court to replace half the people’s land taxes. The emperor commanded Liu Xiang to seek his method, but after five summons, the prince refused to come. Enraged, the emperor harbored hostile intentions. The prince, unable to resist, entrusted Liu Xiang with the cinnabar script, which Liu tied to his elbow. That night, he knocked at the palace gate, believing the elixir could be completed. After several years, the elixir failed, wasting vast sums, for he had not received the oral transmission—it was but empty words on paper. The emperor, furious, sought to punish him. The prince’s ministers, Lei Bei and Wu Bei, whom he had long favored, were sparring with the crown prince with swords when Lei Bei accidentally wounded the prince’s left thigh. Enraged, the prince refused Lei Bei’s request to join the campaign against the Xiongnu to atone for his crime and sought to execute him. Fearing death, Lei Bei reported the prince’s treason to the emperor. Out of familial affection, the emperor hesitated to punish him, merely stripping him of two counties. Wu Bei, meanwhile, had committed private misdeeds and incurred the prince’s wrath, though no action was taken. Wu Bei, fearing execution, corroborated Lei Bei’s earlier accusation of treason. The廷尉 tortured the prince’s ministers until they confessed, fabricating a confession that the treason was real. Sima Qian included this in the *Records of the Grand Historian: Hereditary House of Huainan*, suppressing the fantastical tales of divine transcendence and flying ascent. The emperor then dispatched the宗正 with the imperial staff to punish the prince. The Eight Masters arrived and said to the prince: “The harm caused by Lei Bei and Wu Bei is truly Heaven’s way of urging you on. Now that your Dao is accomplished, you cannot remain long among men, lest you be slandered by ministers. As a subject who deceives his lord and father, Heaven’s law demands your life.” Thereupon, they prepared a wooden effigy, feigning execution. They suspended the prince’s cap and robes from a beam with a wooden pestle, then ascended a mountain with him to perform a great sacrifice. They buried gold in the earth, and the entire household ascended to Heaven in broad daylight. When the宗正 arrived, he saw the prince’s corpse hanging in the courtyard. Suddenly, a report came: “He is not truly dead.” The prince and his family had fled to the mountains of Huainan, ascending to Heaven in broad daylight. The宗正 pursued to the spot but heard only orioles singing in the sky and dogs barking among the clouds. He returned to report to the court. The emperor, filled with regret, executed Lei Bei and Wu Bei, fulfilling the Eight Masters’ words. The *Records of the Grand Historian* records that the prince committed suicide, concealing the tale of his ascension lest later rulers, enamored of the methods of divine transcendence and flying ascent, abandon their sacred duties. Lei Bei and Wu Bei were the prince’s ministers, the true criminals who slandered him. Later generations, unaware of the Eight Masters’ names, mistakenly included the two traitors among them. This account is thus recorded to correct the error.

Eight Salivas:
The outer edges beyond the Nine Provinces:

The *Hong* of the Northeast is called Barren Land,
The *Hong* of the East is called Mulberry Wilds,

The *Hong* of the South is called Reverse Doors,

Two White Paths, Two Black Paths,
Together with the Yellow Path, making Nine Paths.

The Nine Cycles of Returning Elixir:
First cycle in the eleventh month,
Second cycle in the twelfth month,
Third cycle in the first month,
Fourth cycle in the third month,
Fifth cycle in the fourth month,
Sixth cycle in the fifth month,
Seventh cycle in the sixth month,
Eighth cycle in the seventh month,
Ninth cycle in the eighth month.

Alternatively stated:
First cycle descends the Elixir,
Second cycle conjoins the Elixir,
Third cycle nurtures Yang Elixir,
Fourth cycle nurtures Yin Elixir,
Fifth cycle transforms the bones’ Elixir,
Sixth cycle transforms the flesh’ Elixir,
Seventh cycle transforms the Elixir of the Five Viscera and Six Bowels,
Eighth cycle fosters the Fire Elixir,
Ninth cycle ascends the Flying Elixir.

The Nine Cauldrons of Divine Empyrean:
Cauldron of Supreme Ultimate Flying Clouds and Kalpas,

Cauldron of Primordial Chaos,
Cauldron of Floating Radiance and Grotto Heaven,
Cauldron of Numinous Radiance and Spirit Refinement,
Cauldron of Azure Tortoise, Great Serpent, Insects, Fish, and Golden Wheel.

The Nine Difficulties in Cultivating Immortality:
First, the constraint of clothing and food;
Second, the obstruction of elders and superiors;

Third, the entanglement of affection and love;
Fourth, the fetters of fame and profit;
Fifth, the sudden onset of calamities;
Sixth, the violation of the master’s precepts;
Seventh, the divergence of opinions and judgments;
Eighth, the slackening of will and resolve;
Ninth, the wasting of days and months.

Nine Perils in Pursuing the Dao:
Aspiration without opportunity,
Opportunity without companions,
Companions without aspiration,
Aspiration without encountering a master,
Encountering a master without awakening,
Awakening to the master without diligence,
Diligence without upholding the Dao,
Upholding the Dao without steadfastness,
Steadfastness without enduring long.

One White, Kan due north Two Black,
Kun southwest Three Green,
Zhen due east Four Green,
Xun southeast Five Yellow,
Central Six White,
Qian northwest Seven Red,
Dui due west Eight White,
Gen northeast Nine Purple.
Li due south.

Southeast is called Divine Region,
Due south is called Secondary Region,
Southwest is called Martial Region,
Due west is called Gathered Region,
Central is called Ji Region,
Northwest is called Encompassing Region,
Due north is called Mysterious Region,

Lord of the Zhe River,
Lord of the Yangzi River,
Lord of the Song River,

The Offering of Sacrificial Items
According to the *Tongling Miyao*, the names of sacrificial offerings for the jiao rites are listed as follows:
Dried white magpie with water bamboo shoots;
Mulberry moths;
Dried monkey with fragrant mushrooms;

Dried chicken with wood ear mushrooms;
Dried white elephant with lotus seeds;
Dried white horse with coltsfoot flowers;
Dried dragon with wheat;
Dried deer with ox tripe;
Dried lightning from the sea with rhubarb;
Dried mountain boar with water spinach;
Dried "knowing-intestines" with plantain seeds;
Dried marrow from forest horses with sour jujubes;
Dried sprouts with mountain-enclosed red berries;
Dried fish from water with lotus roots;
Dried green caltrop with lily bulbs;
Dried white meat with camphor willow;
Dried earth with sweet flag;
Dried mountain deer with elk;
Fine-scaled fish;
Oil-and-honey cakes;
Great sacrifice ox;
Lesser sacrifice sheep;
Celestial wine and spring water.

Great broth—meat juice. Unseasoned, without the washing of plums. In the earliest antiquity, when the raw first transformed into the rank, meat was merely boiled and its juice drunk, without knowledge of blending flavors. Later generations, revering antiquity in their sacrifices, thus presented only meat juice, calling it *great broth*.

Mysterious water—at all sacrificial rites, when wine vessels are arrayed, mysterious water is placed above the three wines. This exaltation of mysterious water signifies reverence for antiquity, setting the vessel foremost.

*Yu-zeng*—the Zhou people esteemed libations, using *yu* and *zao* combined. True yin reaches the deep springs; the libation is poured with jade tablets, employing the qi of jade.

Straw dogs—objects for praying to heaven and beseeching rain, existing before the Three Dynasties.

The foods used are all the same as those of the secular world, except for wine, tea, pepper-blossom wine, *tusu* wine, thousand-day wine, thousand-league wine, and tofu, all of which originated in the Daoist tradition.

Wine—*The Inner Transmission of the Yellow Emperor* states: The Queen Mother met the Emperor at Mount Song, offering him wine to protect the spirit, nourish qi, preserve the fullness of fluids, and flow with radiance, as well as wine to extend vast longevity and luminous life. Thus, wine already existed in the time of the Yellow Emperor. Yet it remains unknown in which era Du Kang lived, though from ancient times to the present, many have claimed he first created wine.

*Tusu* wine—*Tusu*, as recorded in the *Erya*, is the name of Sun Simiao’s hermitage, signifying the eradication of ghostly qi and the awakening of human souls. The True Man Sun first devised it. Its food offerings are the same as those for pepper-blossom wine.

**Pepper-Blossom Wine**—*Records of the Seasons* states: On New Year’s Day, pepper-blossom wine is offered. Pepper is the essence of the Jade Balance Star; consuming it makes the body light and fleet of foot, prolonging life and enhancing longevity. The order of serving the wine is determined by age, with the eldest first.

**Thousand-Day Wine**—Liu Xuanshi of Zhongshan purchased thousand-day wine and fell into a slumber lasting a thousand days.

**Thousand-League Wine**—Liu Yao of Liang records: In Chenxiang of Guiyang, there was a thousand-league wine; upon drinking it, one would arrive home intoxicated, beginning from the village itself.

**Tea**—During the reign of King Zhao of Zhou, Laozi departed through the Hangu Pass. Yin Xi welcomed him to his home and first offered *ming*, marking the origin of tea. Laozi said: "Those who consume this tea are all disciples of your Dao." Later, it became customary that whenever guests arrived at a household, tea was served first—this was its beginning. *Ming* is tea. Its names are: first *tu* (tea), second *jia*, third *she*, fourth *ming*, and fifth *chuan*.

**Tofu**—The Prince of Huainan attained the Dao of soaring transformation, refining the five metals into treasures and transmuting the eight minerals into water. Having mastered the principles of plant alchemy, he created tofu. At that time, a *dou* of beans in Chang’an was worth a thousand coins. Today, those who observe vegetarian fasts all use it. A poem says: "The whole household learned the arts of Huainan’s guard." The consumption of tofu by later generations began with the Prince of Huainan.

**Tortoise-Peach**—The Yellow Emperor offered *mian* as tortoise-peach in his sacrifices to Heaven, symbolizing the offerings of immortals. Thereafter, all who performed vegetarian rites and jiao ceremonies used it, beginning with the Yellow Emperor.

**Birthday Celebrations and Poison-Averting**—Qian Keng presented incense and a pheasant stew on Yao’s birthday, along with a handkerchief, to celebrate Yao’s longevity. Yao enfeoffed Keng as Lord of Pengcheng. The custom of exchanging handkerchiefs to celebrate birthdays began with this. The compilation of this book removes superfluous passages, awaiting presentation at the celestial gates.

All lesser officials under the Southern Culmen who publish and circulate this book shall have their transgressions pardoned, merits recorded with one rank of advancement, lifespan extended by one *ji* upon their destined allotment, and blessings flourishing for three generations.

**The Jade Register of the Heavenly Emperor’s Supreme Dao and Great Purity, Lower Scroll**—Concluded.
